Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together. 

021004,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021005,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021006,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
021007,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
021008,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
021009,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
021010,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
021011,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
021012,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
021013,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
021014,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021015,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021016,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
021017,000015:                                                                                                  ##              12/01/03 RSB.   Entered/corrected the previously-missing code from
021018,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
021019,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.

021031,000029:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021032,000030: 
021033,000031:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021034,000032: 
021035,000033:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021036,000034:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021037,000035: 
021038,000036:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021039,000037: 
021040,000038:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021041,000039:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021042,000040:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021043,000041:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021044,000042: 
021045,000043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021046,000044: 
021047,000045:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021048,000046: 
021049,000047:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021050,000048: 
021051,000049:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021052,000050:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021053,000051:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021054,000052:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021055,000053:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021056,000054:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021057,000055:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021058,000056:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021059,000057:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021060,000058:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021061,000059: 
021062,000060:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021063,000061: 
021064,000062:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021065,000063:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021066,000064: 
021067,000065:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021068,000066: 
021069,000067:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021070,000068: 
021071,000069:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021072,000070: 
021073,000071:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021074,000072: 
021075,000073:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021076,000074: 
021077,000075:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021078,000076: 
021079,000077:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021080,000078: 
021081,000079:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021082,000080: 
021083,000081:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021084,000082: 
021085,000083: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021086,000084: 
021087,000085: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021088,000086: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021089,000087: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021090,000088: 
021091,000089: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

021499,000497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021500,000498: 
021501,000499:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021502,000500:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021503,000501:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021504,000502: 
021505,000503:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021506,000504: 
021507,000505:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021508,000506:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021509,000507:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021510,000508:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021511,000509: 
021512,000510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021513,000511: 
021514,000512:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021515,000513: 
021516,000514:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021517,000515: 
021518,000516:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP

021521,000519:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC

021526,000524:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021588,000586:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021589,000587:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021590,000588: 
021591,000589:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021592,000590:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021593,000591: 
021594,000592:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021595,000593: 
021596,000594:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021597,000595:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021598,000596: 
021599,000597:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021600,000598: 
021601,000599:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021602,000600:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021603,000601: 
021604,000602:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021605,000603: 
021606,000604:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021607,000605:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021608,000606:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021609,000607: 
021610,000608:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021611,000609: 
021612,000610:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA

Page 512 

021808,000806:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021809,000807:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021810,000808: 
021811,000809:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021812,000810:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021813,000811: 
021814,000812:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021815,000813: 
021816,000814:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021817,000815:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021818,000816: 
021819,000817:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021820,000818: 
021821,000819:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021822,000820:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021823,000821: 
021824,000822:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021825,000823: 
021826,000824:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021827,000825:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021828,000826:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021829,000827:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021830,000828: 
021831,000829:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021832,000830:                                                                                                  #        
021833,000831:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021834,000832:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021835,000833: 
021836,000834:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021837,000835: 
021838,000836:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021839,000837:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021840,000838:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021841,000839: 
021842,000840:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021843,000841: 
021844,000842:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021845,000843: 
021846,000844:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021847,000845: 
021848,000846:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021849,000847: 
021850,000848:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021851,000849: 
021852,000850:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021853,000851: 
021854,000852:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021855,000853: 
021856,000854:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021857,000855: 
021858,000856: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021859,000857: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021860,000858: 24,2675           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021861,000859: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND                                         
021862,000860: 24,2677           03012                           WAND     CHAN12

022034,001032:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022035,001033:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022036,001034: 
022037,001035:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022038,001036:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022039,001037: 
022040,001038:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022041,001039: 
022042,001040:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022043,001041: 
022044,001042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022045,001043: 
022046,001044:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022047,001045: 
022048,001046:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022049,001047: 
022050,001048:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022051,001049:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022052,001050: 
022053,001051:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022054,001052: 
022055,001053:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022056,001054:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022057,001055:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022058,001056: 
022059,001057:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022060,001058: 
022061,001059:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022062,001060: 
022063,001061:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022064,001062: 
022065,001063:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022066,001064: 
022067,001065:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022068,001066: 
022069,001067:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)

022071,001069: 24,3137     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET

022118,001116:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022119,001117:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022120,001118: 
022121,001119:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022122,001120:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022123,001121: 
022124,001122:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022125,001123: 
022126,001124:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022127,001125:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022128,001126:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022129,001127: 
022130,001128:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022131,001129: 
022132,001130:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022133,001131:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022134,001132:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022135,001133:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022136,001134: 
022137,001135:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022138,001136: 
022139,001137:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022140,001138:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022141,001139:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022142,001140: 
022143,001141:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022144,001142: 
022145,001143:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022146,001144:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022147,001145:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022148,001146: 
022149,001147:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022150,001148: 
022151,001149:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022152,001150: 
022153,001151:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022154,001152: 
022155,001153:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022156,001154: 
022157,001155:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022158,001156: 
022159,001157:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022160,001158: 
022161,001159:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022162,001160: 
022163,001161:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022164,001162: 
022165,001163: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022166,001164: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022167,001165: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022168,001166: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022169,001167: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022170,001168: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022171,001169: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022172,001170: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022173,001171: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022174,001172: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022175,001173: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022176,001174: 24,3221           04022                           OCT      04022

022234,001232:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM

022463,001461:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022464,001462: 
022465,001463:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022466,001464: 
022467,001465:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022468,001466:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022469,001467:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022470,001468:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022471,001469:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022472,001470: 
022473,001471:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022474,001472:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022475,001473:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022476,001474:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022477,001475: 
022478,001476:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022479,001477:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022480,001478:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022481,001479:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022482,001480:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022483,001481: 
022484,001482:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022485,001483: 
022486,001484:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022487,001485:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022488,001486: 
022489,001487:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022490,001488: 
022491,001489:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022492,001490:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022493,001491:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022494,001492: 
022495,001493:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022496,001494: 
022497,001495:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022498,001496: 
022499,001497:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022500,001498:

022547,001545:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022548,001546: 
022549,001547:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022550,001548:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022551,001549:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022552,001550:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022553,001551:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022554,001552:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022555,001553:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022556,001554:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022557,001555:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022558,001556:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022559,001557:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022560,001558:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022561,001559:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022562,001560:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022563,001561:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022564,001562:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022565,001563:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022566,001564:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022567,001565:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022568,001566:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022569,001567:

022619,001617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022620,001618: 
022621,001619:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022622,001620: 
022623,001621:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022624,001622:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022625,001623:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022626,001624:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022627,001625:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022628,001626:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022629,001627:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022630,001628:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022631,001629:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022632,001630:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022633,001631:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022634,001632:                                                                                                  #        TC TASKOVER.
022635,001633: 
022636,001634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022637,001635:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022638,001636:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022639,001637: 
022640,001638:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022641,001639: 
022642,001640:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022643,001641: 
022644,001642:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR

022668,001666:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022669,001667: 
022670,001668:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022671,001669: 
022672,001670:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022673,001671:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022674,001672:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022675,001673:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022676,001674:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022677,001675:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022678,001676:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022679,001677:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022680,001678:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022681,001679:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022682,001680:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022683,001681:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022684,001682:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022685,001683:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022686,001684:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022687,001685: 
022688,001686:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022689,001687: 
022690,001688:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022691,001689: 
022692,001690:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022693,001691: 
022694,001692:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022695,001693: 
022696,001694:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_

022699,001697:

022701,001699: 
022702,001700:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022703,001701:

022707,001705: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022745,001743:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022746,001744: 
022747,001745:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022748,001746: 
022749,001747:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022750,001748:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022751,001749:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022752,001750:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022753,001751:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022754,001752:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022755,001753:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022756,001754:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022757,001755:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022758,001756:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022759,001757:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022760,001758:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022761,001759:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022762,001760:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022763,001761:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022764,001762:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022765,001763:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022766,001764:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022767,001765:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022768,001766:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022769,001767:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022770,001768:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022771,001769: 
022772,001770:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022773,001771: 
022774,001772:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022775,001773:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022776,001774: 
022777,001775:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022778,001776: 
022779,001777:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022780,001778: 
022781,001779:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022782,001780: 
022783,001781:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022784,001782: 
022785,001783:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022786,001784: 
022787,001785:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022788,001786: 
022789,001787:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022790,001788: 
022791,001789:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022792,001790: 
022793,001791: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022794,001792: 
022795,001793:                                                                                                  #  ALARM 501 DELETED IN DANCE 279 PER PCR 97.

022838,001836:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022839,001837: 
022840,001838:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022841,001839:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022842,001840:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022843,001841:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022844,001842:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022845,001843:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022846,001844:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022847,001845:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022848,001846:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022849,001847:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022850,001848:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022851,001849:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022852,001850:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022853,001851:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022854,001852:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022855,001853:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022856,001854:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022857,001855:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022858,001856:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022859,001857:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022860,001858: 
022861,001859:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022862,001860: 
022863,001861:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022864,001862:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022865,001863:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022866,001864:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022867,001865: 
022868,001866:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022869,001867: 
022870,001868:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022871,001869: 
022872,001870:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022873,001871: 
022874,001872:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022875,001873: 
022876,001874:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022877,001875: 
022878,001876:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022879,001877: 
022880,001878:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE

022934,001932:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022935,001933: 
022936,001934:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022937,001935: 
022938,001936:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022939,001937:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022940,001938:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022941,001939:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022942,001940:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022943,001941:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022944,001942:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022945,001943:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022946,001944:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022947,001945:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022948,001946:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022949,001947:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022950,001948:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022951,001949:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022952,001950: 
022953,001951:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022954,001952:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022955,001953:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022956,001954:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022957,001955:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022958,001956: 
022959,001957:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022960,001958: 
022961,001959:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022962,001960: 
022963,001961:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022964,001962: 
022965,001963:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022966,001964: 
022967,001965:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022968,001966: 
022969,001967:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022970,001968: 
022971,001969:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022972,001970: 
022973,001971:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
022974,001972:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
022975,001973:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
022976,001974:

023026,002024:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023027,002025: 
023028,002026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023029,002027: 
023030,002028:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023031,002029:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023032,002030:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023033,002031:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023034,002032:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023035,002033:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023036,002034:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023037,002035:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023038,002036:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023039,002037:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023040,002038:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023041,002039:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023042,002040:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023043,002041: 
023044,002042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023045,002043:                                                                                                  #        
023046,002044:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023047,002045:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023136,002134:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023137,002135: 
023138,002136:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023139,002137: 
023140,002138:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023141,002139:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023142,002140:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023143,002141:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023144,002142:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023145,002143:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023146,002144:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023147,002145:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023148,002146:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023149,002147:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023150,002148:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023151,002149:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023152,002150:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023153,002151:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023154,002152:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023155,002153:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023156,002154:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023157,002155:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023158,002156:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023159,002157:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023160,002158:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023161,002159:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023162,002160: 
023163,002161:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023164,002162: 
023165,002163:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023166,002164:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023167,002165:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023168,002166:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023169,002167: 
023170,002168:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023171,002169: 
023172,002170:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023173,002171: 
023174,002172:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023175,002173: 
023176,002174:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023177,002175:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023178,002176: 
023179,002177:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023180,002178: 
023181,002179:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023182,002180: 
023183,002181:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023184,002182: 
023185,002183:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023186,002184:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023187,002185:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
023188,002186:

023226,002224:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023227,002225: 
023228,002226:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023229,002227:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023230,002228:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023231,002229:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023232,002230:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023233,002231:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023234,002232:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023235,002233:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023236,002234:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023237,002235:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023238,002236:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023239,002237:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023240,002238:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023241,002239:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023242,002240:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023243,002241:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023244,002242:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023245,002243:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023246,002244:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023247,002245:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023248,002246:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
