023399,002397:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023400,002398: 
023401,002399:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023402,002400:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023403,002401:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023404,002402:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023405,002403:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023406,002404:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023407,002405:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023408,002406:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023409,002407:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023410,002408:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023411,002409:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023412,002410:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023413,002411:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023414,002412:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023415,002413:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023416,002414:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023417,002415:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023418,002416:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023419,002417:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023420,002418:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023421,002419:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023422,002420:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023423,002421:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023424,002422:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023425,002423:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023426,002424:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023427,002425: 
023428,002426:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023429,002427: 
023430,002428:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023431,002429:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023432,002430:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023433,002431: 
023434,002432:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023435,002433:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023436,002434: 
023437,002435:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023438,002436:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDMAC
023439,002437: 
023440,002438:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023441,002439: 
023442,002440:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023443,002441:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023444,002442: 
023445,002443:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023446,002444:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023447,002445:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023448,002446: 
023449,002447: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023494,002492:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023495,002493: 
023496,002494:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023497,002495: 
023498,002496:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023499,002497:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023500,002498:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023501,002499:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023502,002500:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023503,002501:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023504,002502:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023505,002503:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023506,002504:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023507,002505:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023508,002506:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023509,002507:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023510,002508:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023511,002509:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023512,002510:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023513,002511:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023514,002512:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023515,002513:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023516,002514:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023517,002515:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023518,002516:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023519,002517:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023520,002518:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023521,002519:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023522,002520:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023523,002521:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023524,002522:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023525,002523:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023526,002524:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023527,002525:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023528,002526:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023529,002527:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023530,002528:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023531,002529:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023532,002530:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023533,002531:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023534,002532:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023535,002533: 
023536,002534:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023537,002535: 
023538,002536:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023539,002537: 
023540,002538:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023541,002539: 
023542,002540:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023543,002541:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023544,002542: 
023545,002543:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023546,002544: 
023547,002545:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 552 

023549,002547: 
023550,002548:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023551,002549: 
023552,002550:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023553,002551: 
023554,002552:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023555,002553: 
023556,002554:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023557,002555: 
023558,002556: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023559,002557: 25,2647           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023560,002558: 25,2650           53107                           DXCH     TANG

023612,002610:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A
023613,002611:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023619,002617: 25,2731           40110                           CS       RADMODES                              #  A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES POLARITY OF
023620,002618: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023621,002619: 25,2733           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT
023622,002620: 25,2734           12737                           BZF      +3                                    #  GYRO CAUSES A POSITIVE CHANGE IN THE
023623,002621: 25,2735           31107                           CA       TANG       +1                         #  SHAFT ANGLE.  COMPENSATE FOR THIS SWITCH

024235,003233:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.

024360,003358:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024361,003359:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024362,003360: 
024363,003361:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024364,003362:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024365,003363:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024366,003364:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024367,003365:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024368,003366: 
024369,003367:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024370,003368: 
024371,003369:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024372,003370:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024373,003371:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024374,003372:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024375,003373:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024376,003374: 
024377,003375:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024378,003376: 
024379,003377:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024380,003378:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024381,003379:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024382,003380: 
024383,003381:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024384,003382:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024385,003383: 
024386,003384:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024387,003385:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024388,003386: 
024389,003387:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024390,003388:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024391,003389:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024392,003390:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024393,003391:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,ADG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024394,003392:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024395,003393: 
024396,003394:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024397,003395:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 575 

024399,003397:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024400,003398:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024401,003399:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024402,003400: 
024403,003401:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST

024533,003531:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)
024534,003532:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P VOLANTE  SDC              DATE   4-11-67
024535,003533: 
024536,003534:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024537,003535:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS
024538,003536:

024540,003538:

024544,003542: 
024545,003543:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXIT -  RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO 00001 - RADAR LOS NOT WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF LM +Z AXIS
024546,003544:

024551,003549:                                                                                                  #        RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024552,003550:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 - INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024553,003551: 
024554,003552:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS - A,L,Q MPAC - PUSHLIST AND PUSHLOC ARE NOT CHANGED BY THIS ROUTINE

024584,003582:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024585,003583:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024586,003584:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024587,003585: 
024588,003586:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024589,003587:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024590,003588:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024591,003589:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024592,003590: 
024593,003591:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024594,003592:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024595,003593:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024596,003594:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024597,003595:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024598,003596:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024599,003597:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024600,003598: 
024601,003599:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024602,003600:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024603,003601:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024604,003602: 
024605,003603:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024606,003604:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024607,003605:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024608,003606:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024609,003607:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024610,003608:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024611,003609: 
024612,003610:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024613,003611:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024614,003612:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024615,003613:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024616,003614:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024617,003615:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024618,003616:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024619,003617:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024620,003618:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024621,003619:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024622,003620:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024623,003621:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024624,003622:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024625,003623:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024626,003624:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024627,003625: 
024628,003626:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024629,003627:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024630,003628:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

024632,003630:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

025021,004019: 
025022,004020:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025023,004021:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025024,004022:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025025,004023:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025026,004024: 
025027,004025:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025028,004026:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025029,004027:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025030,004028: 
025031,004029:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025032,004030:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025033,004031:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025034,004032:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025035,004033:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025036,004034:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 589 

025038,004036: 
025039,004037:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025040,004038:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025041,004039:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025042,004040:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025043,004041:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025044,004042:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025045,004043:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
025046,004044: 
025047,004045: 26,3200           77624        LSR22.4            CALL

025154,004152:                                                                                                  #  GETULC

025184,004182:

025246,004244:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025247,004245:                                                                                                  #  MCD NO  0                     BY P VOLANTE  SDC               DATE 1-15-67
025248,004246: 
025249,004247:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025250,004248: 
025251,004249:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025252,004250:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025253,004251:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025254,004252:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025255,004253: 
025256,004254:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025257,004255: 
025258,004256:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025259,004257: 
025260,004258:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025261,004259:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025262,004260:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025263,004261:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025264,004262:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025265,004263: 
025266,004264:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025267,004265: 
025268,004266:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025269,004267: 
025270,004268:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025271,004269:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025272,004270:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   - FOR DISPLAY IN R2 -     ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025273,004271: 
025274,004272:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025275,004273: 
025276,004274:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025277,004275:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025278,004276: 
025279,004277:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025280,004278: 
025281,004279:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025282,004280:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025283,004281:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025284,004282:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025285,004283:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025286,004284: 
025287,004285: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025288,004286: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025289,004287: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025290,004288: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025291,004289: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025499,004497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025500,004498:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025501,004499: 
025502,004500:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025503,004501: 
025504,004502:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025505,004503:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025506,004504:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025507,004505:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025508,004506:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025509,004507:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025510,004508: 
025511,004509:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025512,004510: 
025513,004511:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025514,004512: 
025515,004513:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025516,004514:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025517,004515:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025518,004516:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025519,004517:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025520,004518:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025521,004519: 
025522,004520:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025523,004521: 
025524,004522:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025525,004523: 
025526,004524:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025527,004525:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025528,004526:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025529,004527:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025530,004528:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 600 

025532,004530: 
025533,004531:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025534,004532: 
025535,004533:                                                                                                  #        NCR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025536,004534:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025537,004535:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025538,004536:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025539,004537: 
025540,004538:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025541,004539: 
025542,004540:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025543,004541:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025544,004542:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025545,004543:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025546,004544: 
025547,004545:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025548,004546: 
025549,004547:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025550,004548: 
025551,004549:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE:  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025552,004550:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025553,004551:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025554,004552: 
025555,004553: 33,2045                                           BANK     33

025559,004557: 33,2045                                           COUNT*   $$/r29

025655,004653:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN
025656,004654:                                                                                                  #  START IT UP WHEN THE DATA IS IN PLACE.

025659,004657: 33,2141           03527                                    V                                     #  LOSVEL = V(CSM) - V.

025661,004659: 33,2143           52255                           VAD      VSU                                   #        AND ADD THE RESULT TO R(CSM) - R TO GET

Page 605 

025728,004726:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025729,004727: 
025730,004728:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025731,004729:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025732,004730:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025733,004731:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025734,004732:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025735,004733: 
025736,004734:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025737,004735:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025738,004736: 
025739,004737: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025740,004738: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025741,004739: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025742,004740: 
025743,004741: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025744,004742: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025745,004743: 
025746,004744: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025747,004745: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025748,004746: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025749,004747: 
025750,004748: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025751,004749: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025752,004750: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025753,004751: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025754,004752:
